1249<h1 class="sc-1qt2sb7-0 sc-1jm2530-3 izaALp">

1250Why our program could be right for you </h1>

1251<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 sc-1jm2530-5 WqZms">

1252<p>

1253Our comprehensive program combines a first-rate clinical experience with outstanding laboratory and translational research opportunities. Training in the diverse borough of the Bronx, our residents experience a wide range of cancer pathologies and develop the skills needed to become independent expert practitioners. Using state-of-the-art technology, residents train across all areas of radiation oncology, including brachytherapy, stereotactic radiation, intraoperative radiation and proton therapy.&nbsp;</p>

1283<h1 class="sc-1qt2sb7-0 sc-1jm2530-3 izaALp">

1284What sets Montefiore Einstein apart</h1>

1285<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 sc-1jm2530-5 WqZms">

1286<p>

1287<span>

1288<span>

1289<span>

1290<span>

1291<span>

1292<span>

1293At Montefiore Einstein, we are guided by a mission to heal, to teach, to discover and to advance the health of the communities we serve. Comprising 11 member hospitals and more than 200 specialty care sites, Montefiore Health System provides highly specialized, coordinated care for diverse populations in the New York region, across the country and globally.</span>

1294</span>

1295</span>

1296</span>

1297</span>

1298</span>

1299</p>

1300

1301

1303<span>

1304<span>

1305<span>

1306<span>

1307<span>

1308<span>

1309Albert Einstein College of Medicine, home to nearly 1,000 students in its MD, PhD and combined MD/PhD programs, is one of the nation’s preeminent centers for research, medical education and clinical investigation. Through the joint efforts of Montefiore Health System and Albert Einstein College of Medicine, Montefiore Einstein is able to advance research and accelerate discoveries, benefiting patients and ensuring access to state-of-the-art healthcare for all. &nbsp;</span>

1363<h1 class="sc-1qt2sb7-0 sc-1jm2530-3 izaALp">

1364Graduate Medical Education at Montefiore Einstein </h1>

1365<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 sc-1jm2530-5 WqZms">

1366<p>

1367Representing one of the top 10 largest medical and surgical training programs in the country, Montefiore Health System and our Albert Einstein College of Medicine provide postgraduate clinical training to more than 1,400 residents and fellows per year. Clinicians across Montefiore Einstein’s numerous educational programs actively mentor and cultivate a new generation of healthcare leaders.&nbsp;</p>

1368

1369

1370<p>

1371Our mission to improve access and quality of care for our diverse community draws residents and fellows from top medical, dental and PA schools from around the world. We develop and expand programs designed to advance teamwork, communication and decision-making, and our progressive focus on comprehensive care provides an ideal training ground for our residents and fellows.</p>

1372

1373

1374<p>

1375To make the process of working and training at Montefiore Einstein more seamless, we offer a variety of services for our house staff, physician assistants and interns, including assistance with credentialing and orientation, institutional resources, visas, contracts, HR documents, payroll, notary services and specialty training and certifications.&nbsp;</p>

1376

1377</div>

1631<section class="hd9hse-0 MediaCarousel__Container-e7xgl7-0 hvnMUj">

1634<h1 class="MediaCarousel__Headline-e7xgl7-1 cZPexe">

1635An ambulatory surgery center and specialty care location </h1>

1636<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 MediaCarousel__CopyText-e7xgl7-2 eJyYfj">

1637<p>

1638Home to our ambulatory surgery center, Hutchinson Campus is Montefiore Einstein’s newest facility. While training here, residents perform gynecologic, prostate and breast brachytherapy procedures. Residents also gain experience with an intraoperative radiation therapy (IORT) technique that uses the Zeiss Intrabeam System to deliver precise radiation directly to the tumor bed, allowing breast cancer patients to receive radiation treatment in the operating room at the time of surgery.</p>

1699<h1 class="sc-1qt2sb7-0 HeroMediaBlock__FooterTitle-sc-3qeyiq-15 ecldOG">

1700New York Proton Center </h1>

1701</div>

1702</div>

1703</section>

1706</section>

1707<section class="hd9hse-0 MediaCarousel__Container-e7xgl7-0 jaySAo">

1708<div class="MediaCarousel__Row-e7xgl7-4 hhYQrM">

1709<div>

1710<h1 class="MediaCarousel__Headline-e7xgl7-1 cZPexe">

1711A founding partner in New York&#x27;s first and only proton center</h1>

1712<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 MediaCarousel__CopyText-e7xgl7-2 eJyYfj">

1713<p>

1714Montefiore Einstein has long recognized the value of proton therapy, which is why we established an alliance with the area’s only proton therapy center, in 2012. This alliance enabled our specialists to offer proton therapy to patients, years before most other cancer centers in the nation. In 2019, Montefiore Einstein became a founding partner of the New York Proton Center, the first of its kind in New York City. We now have 23 Montefiore Einstein physicists and 13 physicians treating patients at this facility.</p>

1715

1716</div>

1746<div>

1747<h1 class="MediaCarousel__Headline-e7xgl7-1 cZPexe">

1748Site of our Hematology-Oncology Outpatient Practice </h1>

1749<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 MediaCarousel__CopyText-e7xgl7-2 eJyYfj">

1750<p>

1751Chandan Guha, MD, and colleagues in his Montefiore Einstein research lab were early investigators of radiation-enhanced tumor vaccines which amplify the tumor immune response using conventional and exploratory cancer therapies. Their research focus also includes the development of stem cell-based therapies for the mitigation of acute radiation syndrome and radiation-induced gastrointestinal syndrome resulting from radiation injury, as well as preparative live irradiation for hepatocyte transplant in acute liver injury and cirrhosis in place of liver transplant.</p>

2138<section id="curriculum" class="hd9hse-0 MediaCarousel__Container-e7xgl7-0 jaySAo">

2139<div class="MediaCarousel__Row-e7xgl7-4 hhYQrM">

2140<div>

2141<h1 class="MediaCarousel__Headline-e7xgl7-1 cZPexe">

2142A challenging and innovative curriculum </h1>

2143<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 MediaCarousel__CopyText-e7xgl7-2 eJyYfj">

2144<p>

2145While training at Montefiore Einstein, residents enhance their skills under the guidance of expert faculty members who specialize in treating central nervous system cancer and metastases, head and neck cancer, breast cancer, lung cancer, gastrointestinal cancer, genitourinary cancer, gynecologic cancer, bone and soft tissue cancer, skin cancer and pediatric cancer. Residents have the opportunity to take part in interdisciplinary tumor board conferences, as well as participate in specialized radiation treatments and procedures, such as intracavitary and interstitial brachytherapy, stereotactic radiosurgery (SRS), stereotactic body radiation therapy (SBRT), intraoperative radiation therapy (IORT) and proton therapy.</p>

2146

2147</div>

2148</div>

2149<div>

2150</div>

2151</div>

2152</section>

2154<section id="diversity-of-experience" class="hd9hse-0 cAiRaK">

2155<div class="ColumnsCarouselBlock__Divider-gvnrqr-3 eRonrH">

2156</div>

2157<div class="ColumnsCarouselBlock__Header-gvnrqr-9 idecAP">

2158<div>

2159<h1 class="sc-1qt2sb7-0 ColumnsCarouselBlock__ModuleHeadline-gvnrqr-11 iUokce">

2160An unmatched diversity of experience</h1>

2161<h2 class="ColumnsCarouselBlock__ModuleSummary-gvnrqr-12 hsHSlg">

2162As a premier academic medical center serving the Bronx, Westchester and the Hudson Valley, Montefiore Einstein offers its postgraduate trainees comprehensive exposure to a broad diversity of patients and pathologies. The diverse range of experience available prepares our postgraduate trainees for future careers in their chosen field, be it in the research or clinical and/or non-clinical setting. </h2>

2163</div>

2164</div>

2856<div class="sc-10cvvij-2 eDaCnc">

2857<h1 class="sc-1qt2sb7-0 sc-10cvvij-4 ugwjZ">

2858Live and work close to the best of everything</h1>

2859<div data-richtext-component="true" class="q27lov-0 sc-10cvvij-3 rUnIp">

2860<p>

2861The Bronx, New York City’s northernmost borough, is a culturally rich neighborhood placed at the intersection of Manhattan and its surrounding regions. Our postgraduate trainees typically live in hospital housing or off-site in nearby Riverdale, Lower Westchester or Manhattan, and have access to an unmatched diversity of experiences beyond the program itself.&nbsp;</p>

2862

2863

2864<p>

2865In the Bronx, with its ample parks and gardens, you’ll learn first-hand why it’s known as “the City’s Greenest Borough.” The neighborhood offers plenty of local food, art, sports and culture, and is just a subway ride away from Manhattan’s famed theaters, museums and attractions.&nbsp;</p>

2866

2867

2868<p>

2869As a resident of the Tri-State region, you’ll have unmatched access to the city’s cultural offerings, not to mention the bounty of outdoor excursions that are available just beyond. Day-trips and weekend excursions to the Hudson Valley, Catskills, Long Island or New Jersey provide ample opportunities for swimming, hiking, biking, skiing and other seasonal activities.&nbsp;</p>

2870

2871

2872<h4>

2873Drag map or zoom to explore things to do in the Bronx, Manhattan and beyond.&nbsp;</h4>

2874

2875</div>

2876</div>

2887Residency Application Information </h1>

2889<h3>

2890We’re seeking residents who will shape the future of healthcare.</h3>

2891

2892

2893<p>

2894If you would like to apply to become a Radiation Oncology Resident at Montefiore Einstein, here is some information to keep in mind.</p>

2897<ul>

2906September 27, 2023—Residency programs begin reviewing applications</li>

2907

2912March 11-15, 2024—Match week</li>
